<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:leep.html>leep</a> (115721)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leep.html>leep</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leper.html>leper</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">leepst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>crafty, shrewd</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> shifted, tilted</li>
<li>with watery, tearing <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>eyes</a></li></ol>

***leer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:leer.html>leer</a> (1356)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Contraction of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leder.html>leder</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:leder.html>leder</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*lether</i>, from<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*leþrą</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_8">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leer.html>leer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leren.html>leren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leer.html>leertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>leather
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leder.html>leder</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_3">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lêre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">lēra</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*laizō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_9">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leer.html>leer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leren.html>leren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leer.html>leertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>teachings</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:leer.html>leer</a></i>, contraction of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ledere.html>ledere</a></i>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Alternative form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ladder.html>ladder</a></i></span></span>.</li></ol>

***leery.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:leery.html>leery</a> (60271)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>1718, "untrustful, suspicious", either from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:leer.html>leer</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-y</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lear</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">learning, knowledge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-y</i>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:leer.html>leer</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">lear</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:leery.html>leery</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">leerier</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">leeriest</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Cautious, suspicious, wary, hesitant, or nervous about something; having reservations or <a href = vnd.unilang:concerns.html>concerns</a>.
<dl><dd><i>Since he <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bitten.html>bitten</a> by a dog when he <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> young, he <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> always <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:leery.html>leery</a></b> of animals.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
</body>

***leeuwendeel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:leeuwendeel.html>leeuwendeel</a> (56896)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leeuw.html>leeuw</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deel.html>deel</a></i>. After one of Aesop's fables.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leeuwendeel.html>leeuwendeel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leeuwendeel.html>leeuwendelen</a></b>)

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lef.html>lef</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">courage</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gozer.html>gozer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">guy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Someone with a lot of <a href = vnd.unilang:chutzpah.html>chutzpah</a>; a daring or impudent person.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:legende.html>legende</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:legende.html>legende</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:legende.html>legende</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:legenda.html>legenda</a></i>.

***leger.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:leger.html>leger</a> (736)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:leger.html>leger</a></i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*legrą</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leger.html>leger</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:legers.html>legers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:legertje.html>legertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">army</span>, armed forces

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:legger.html>legger</a> (115698)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:legger.html>legger</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leggen.html>leggen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:legger.html>legger</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leggers.html>leggers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:legger.html>leggertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>An animal that lays eggs, especially an egg-producing bird.</li>
<li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">ledger</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">register</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">book for <a href = vnd.unilang:keeping.html>keeping</a> records and/or notes</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">textual criticism</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <span class="Latn" lang="en">vorlage</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">edition of a text that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the immediate predecessor or one of the immediate predecessors of another edition</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li></ol>

***legio.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:legio.html>legio</a> (69067)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">legiō</i>, after the story of <a href = vnd.unilang:legio.html>Legio</a> and the demoniac. The neuter gender in the noun sense “multitude” <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> influenced by the related term <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:legioen.html>legioen</a></i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:legioen.html>legioen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:legio.html>legio</a></strong> (<i>used only predicatively</i>, <i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">legion</span>, numerous</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:legio.html>legio</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:legio.html>legio</a>'s</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <span class="Latn" lang="en">multitude</span>, a <span class="Latn" lang="en">crowd</span>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onze.html>Onze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stad.html>stad</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werd.html>werd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geteisterd.html>geteisterd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:legio.html>legio</a>'s</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ratten.html>ratten</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Our city <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> being plagued by <b>multitudes</b> of <a href = vnd.unilang:rats.html>rats</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:legioen.html>legioen</a></span></li></ul>
<hr />
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:legio.html>legio</a></b>

***legioen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:legioen.html>legioen</a> (10148)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:legioen.html>legioen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">legion</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">legiō</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:legio.html>legio</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:legioen.html>legioen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:legioenen.html>legioenen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:legioen.html>legioentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">often historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">legion</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">major division of an army</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>, especially a Roman legion</li>
<li>large group (of people or animals); a legion</li></ol>

***leguaan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:leguaan.html>leguaan</a> (34978)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es"><a href = vnd.unilang:iguana.html>iguana</a></i>, with assimilation of the Spanish definite article, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ta%C3%ADno_language" class="extiw" title="w:Taíno language">Taíno</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tnq">*iwana</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leguaan.html>leguaan</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leguanen.html>leguanen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leguaan.html>leguaantje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>An <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:iguana.html>iguana</a></span>; lizard of the family Iguanidae; historically also including members of the Iguania.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:leguaan.html>leguaan</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>

***leiden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:leiden.html>leiden</a> (1133)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:leiden.html>leiden</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:leiden.html>leiden</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*laidijan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*laidijaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leiden.html>leiden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lead, to take the lead</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to guide</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lead, to go, to follow a path to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:alle.html>Alle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wegen.html>wegen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:leiden.html>leiden</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rome.html>Rome</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">All roads <b>lead</b> to <a href = vnd.unilang:rome.html>Rome</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***lekken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lekken.html>lekken</a> (10821)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:lekken.html>lekken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lakjaną</i>.
</p><p>The "to lick" sense <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> derived from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lecken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">leckon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*likkōną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lekken.html>lekken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to <span class="Latn" lang="en">leak</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_dialects" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch dialects">Southern</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to <span class="Latn" lang="en">lick</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***lekker.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lekker.html>lekker</a> (370)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lecker</i>, derived from the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:lekken.html>lekken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:likken.html>likken</a></i>). Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">lecker</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Afrikaans" class="extiw" title="w:Afrikaans"><a href = vnd.unilang:afrikaans.html>Afrikaans</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="af"><a href = vnd.unilang:lekker.html>lekker</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">lecker</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no"><a href = vnd.unilang:lekker.html>lekker</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">läcker</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">lækker</i>. More at lick.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_3">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lekker.html>lekker</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lekkerder.html>lekkerder</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lekkerst.html>lekkerst</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Having a nice taste, tasty, delectable.

<li>Good, nice, pleasant in a more generic sense.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:lekker.html>Lekker</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Nice weather!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">attributive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Hot, <a href = vnd.unilang:sexy.html>sexy</a>, physically attractive.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a>'n <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lekker.html>lekker</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ding.html>ding</a>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He's such a hottie!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Hé, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lekkere.html>lekkere</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:meid.html>meid</a>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:hey.html>Hey</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:sexy.html>sexy</a> girl!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">Healthy</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">well</span>, in good health.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:paar.html>paar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:minuten.html>minuten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nadat.html>nadat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:klas.html>klas</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:klaagde.html>klaagde</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:begon.html>begon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:docent.html>docent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lekker.html>lekker</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voelen.html>voelen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">A few minutes after the class complained, the teacher also began to feel un<b>well</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lekkers.html>lekkers</a> (5680)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Partitive form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lekker.html>lekker</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tasty, good</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lekkers.html>lekkers</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>what <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> tasty, <a href = vnd.unilang:sweets.html>sweets</a>, treats
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>Na</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:harde.html>harde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>werken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lekkers.html>lekkers</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:verdiend.html>verdiend</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">After all that hard work they earned themselves something tasty.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wie.html>Wie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zoet.html>zoet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:krijgt.html>krijgt</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lekkers.html>lekkers</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:wie.html>wie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stout.html>stout</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> roe.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> sweet <a href = vnd.unilang:gets.html>gets</a> treats, who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> naughty the rod. <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lilie</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lēlie</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">līlia</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:lilia.html>lilia</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">līlia</i>, the plural of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">līlium</i> that <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> reinterpreted as a singular form.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lelie.html>lelie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lelies.html>lelies</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">leliën</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lelie.html>lelietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:lily.html>lily</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">heraldry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:fleur-de-lis.html>fleur-de-lis</a>, although botanically an <a href = vnd.unilang:iris.html>iris</a></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:lelie.html>lelie</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:plantkunde.html>plantkunde</a>)</span> <i>Liliacecae</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bloem.html>bloem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> plantengeslacht <a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Lilium" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Lilium"><span style="color:green;"><i>Lilium</i></span></a> <img alt="op Wikispecies" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/14px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png" decoding="async" width="14" height="18" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/21px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/28px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 2x" data-file-width="125" data-file-height="160" /></li></ol>

***lelieblank.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lelieblank.html>lelieblank</a> (91282)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lelie.html>lelie</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blank.html>blank</a></i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lily-white</i>, possibly the etymon of the Dutch term. First attested in the early eighteenth century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lelieblank.html>lelieblank</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>lily-white, pale white <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">now mainly referring to (pale) white skin tones</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***lelietje-van-dalen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lelietje-van-dalen.html>lelietje-van-dalen</a> (127918)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">līlium</i> and  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Translingualism" class="extiw" title="w:Translingualism">translingual</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="mul">Convallaria</i>. Literally, “little <a href = vnd.unilang:lily.html>lily</a> of [the] dales”.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lelietje-van-dalen.html>lelietje-van-dalen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lelietjes-van-dalen.html>lelietjes-van-dalen</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:lily.html>lily</a> of the valley (<i>Convallaria majalis</i>)</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">meiklokje</span></li></ul>

***lelijk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lelijk.html>lelijk</a> (2064)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">leetlijc</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lelic</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leed.html>leed</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sorrow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-lijk</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-like</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">lēthlīk</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">leidlīh</i> (but modern German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">leidlich</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tolerable</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not directly related), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs">lēthlik</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">lāðlīc</i> (Modern English <i class="Latn mention" lang="an">loathly</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
